                    - /url: /enterprise-version/#access-palette
                  - text: .

                  - code [ref=e3594]: airgap-pack-aws-alb-2.5.1.bin
                  - text: binary. Replace
                  - code [ref=e3595]: XXXX
                  - text: with your username and
                  - code [ref=e3596]: YYYY
                  - text: with your password.
                - list [ref=e3597]:
                  - listitem [ref=e3598]:
                    - paragraph [ref=e3599]:
                      - text: In your terminal, use the following command template to SSH into the Palette airgap support VM. Enter the path to your private SSH key, username, and the IP or domain of the airgap support VM. The default username is
                      - code [ref=e3600]: ubuntu
                      - text: .

                      - code [ref=e3604]:

                - heading "Conformance CapabilitiesDirect link to Conformance Capabilities" [level=2] [ref=e3688]:
                  - text: Conformance Capabilities
                  - link "Direct link to Conformance Capabilities" [ref=e3689] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: "#conformance-capabilities"
                    - text: "#"
                - paragraph [ref=e3690]:
                  - text: In an airgap installation, you need to upload the conformance packs to the self-hosted OCI registry. The conformance binary contains the packs required to use the
                  - link "Compliance Scan" [ref=e3691] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /clusters/cluster-management/compliance-scan/
                  - text: capabilities. The conformance binary can be found in the
                  - link "Cluster Profile Packs" [ref=e3692] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: "#cluster-profile-packs"
                  - text: table. The binary has the prefix
                  - code [ref=e3693]: airgap-thirdparty-
                  - text: . Follow the
                  - link "Usage Instructions" [ref=e3694] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: "#usage-instructions"
                  - text: to upload the conformance packs to the OCI registry.
